 ENDF/B-VI.8 MF32 rel uncertainties adjusted to the those from    1125 1451   19
 the Atlas of Neutron Resonances [1]. Thermal uncertainties for   1125 1451   20
 capture and elastic were added using file 33. Elastic was set    1125 1451   21
 to 5.5%, as half the difference between the thermal value in     1125 1451   22
 this evaluation and the value in the Atlas. The capture thermal  1125 1451   23
 unc was taken from the Atlas.                                    1125 1451   24
                                                                  1125 1451   25
 In the fast neutron region the sensitivity calculations were     1125 1451   26
 performed with the EMPIRE code. The spherical optical model      1125 1451   27
 provided total cross sections and neutron scattering,            1125 1451   28
 Hauser-Feshbach statistical model described the bulk of particle 1125 1451   29
 emission, and the exciton pre-equilibrium model described major  1125 1451   30
 features of fast particle emission at higher incident energies.  1125 1451   31
 Altogether, 21 model parameters were varied. The Bayesian        1125 1451   32
 update procedure was performed by the KALMAN [2] code by taking  1125 1451   33
 into account the sensitivity calculations and selected           1125 1451   34
 experimental data.                                               1125 1451   35

MF=2                                                              1125 1451   78
   Resonance parameters are used from 600 eV to 500 keV.  The     1125 1451   79
 thermal capture cross section is given as 528 mb, in agreement   1125 1451   80
 with the experimental results of 526.9+-4.5 mb [RY71], as well   1125 1451   81
 as earlier results summarized in [RY71].  Using resonance        1125 1451   82
 parameters E=2.81 keV, GN=376 eV, and GG=0.353 eV for the large  1125 1451   83
 2.81 keV resonance gives the correct thermal capture value using 1125 1451   84
 a Breit-Wigner shape, and this form is used to calculate the     1125 1451   85
 capture crposs section from 1.0E-5 to 600 eV.  The capture       1125 1451   86
 width GG=0.353 eV is consistent with a recent result by Wilson   1125 1451   87
 [WI77] where they find 0.24<GG<0.4 eV with a 90% confidence      1125 1451   88
 level, and with a recent preliminary result of Macklin [MA76]    1125 1451   89
 where he found GG=0.385+-0.04 eV.  The GN and ER values are      1125 1451   90
 taken from Seltzer [SE74].  From 600 eV to 500 keV, the capture  1125 1451   91
 cross section is generated from resonance areas reported by      1125 1451   92
 Musgrove [MU77], and neutron widths and spins obtained from      1125 1451   93
 a multilevel analysis of the transmission data of Larson [LA76]. 1125 1451   94
                                                                  1125 1451   95
MF=3                                                              1125 1451   96
   MT=1  Resonance parameters + data of Larson [LA76].            1125 1451   97
   MT=2  MT=1 - MT=3                                              1125 1451   98
   MT=3  SUM 3/4+3/16+3/102+3/103+3/107                           1125 1451   99
   MT=4  SUM 3/51-68,91                                           1125 1451  100
   MT=102  As discussed above, the shape of the capture cross     1125 1451  101
     section from 1.E-5 eV to 600 eV was taken from a single      1125 1451  102
     level Breit-Wigner form from 600 eV to 500 keV, File 3 gives 1125 1451  103
     no contribution.  From 500 keV to 20 MeV the capture file is 1125 1451  104
     the same as the ENDF/B-IV file by Pitterle and Paik [PI72].  1125 1451  105
   MT=103  Taken from ENDF4 - Modified >8 MeV                     1125 1451  106
     Based on 2 step Hauser-Feshbach calculations                 1125 1451  107
   MT=107  Taken from ENDF/B-IV                                   1125 1451  108
MF=4                                                              1125 1451  109
   MT=2  Taken mainly from [KI76], ENDF/B-IV and Optical Model    1125 1451  110
     calculations. All other angular distributions assumed        1125 1451  111
     isotropic.                                                   1125 1451  112

 are estimated from the literature for the 2.81 keV resonance,    1125 1451  129
